      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Han_character">
        Han character
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%BE%8D&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Han character">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <div class="noprint" style="border:solid #aaa 1px;margin:0;font-size:74%;background:#f9f3f6;width:120px;padding:3px;spacing:0;text-align:center;float:right">
       <div style="float:left">
        <figure class="mw-halign-none" typeof="mw:File">
         <a href="https://commons.wikimedia.org/wiki/Category:Radical_212" title="commons:Category:Radical 212">
          <img data-file-height="1376" data-file-width="1024" decoding="async" height="32" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4a/Commons-logo.svg/24px-Commons-logo.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4a/Commons-logo.svg/36px-Commons-logo.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4a/Commons-logo.svg/48px-Commons-logo.svg.png 2x" width="24"/>
         </a>
         <figcaption>
         </figcaption>
        </figure>
       </div>
       <a class="extiw" href="https://commons.wikimedia.org/wiki/Category:Radical_212-0" title="commons:Category:Radical 212-0">
        See images of
        <br/>
        <b>
         Radical 212
         <big>
          龍
         </big>
        </b>
       </a>
      </div>
      <p>
       <strong class="Hani headword" lang="mul">
        龍
       </strong>
       (
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Kangxi_radical" title="Kangxi radical">
         Kangxi radical
        </a>
        212,
       </i>
       <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Chinese_radical/%E9%BE%8D" title="Appendix:Chinese radical/龍">
        龍
       </a>
       +0, 16 strokes,
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Chinese_Cangjie" title="Appendix:Chinese Cangjie">
         cangjie input
        </a>
       </i>
       卜月卜尸心 (
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Appendix:Chinese_Cangjie/y" title="Appendix:Chinese Cangjie/y">
        YBYSP
       </a>
       ),
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Chinese_four_corner" title="Appendix:Chinese four corner">
         four-corner
        </a>
       </i>
       <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Chinese_four_corner/0" title="Appendix:Chinese four corner/0">
        0121
        <sub>
         1
        </sub>
       </a>
       ,
       <i>
        <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chinese_character_description_languages#Ideographic_Description_Sequences" title="w:Chinese character description languages">
         composition
        </a>
       </i>
       ⿰
       <a href="/wiki/%F0%A6%9A%8F" title="𦚏">
        𦚏
       </a>
       ⿱
       <a href="/wiki/%E2%BA%8A" title="⺊">
        ⺊
       </a>
       ⿷
       <a href="/wiki/%E5%B7%B1" title="己">
        己
       </a>
       <a href="/wiki/%E4%B8%89" title="三">
        三
       </a>
       )
      </p>
      <ol>
       <li>
        <a href="/wiki/Kangxi_radical" title="Kangxi radical">
         Kangxi radical
        </a>
        #212,
        <i class="Hani mention" lang="mul">
         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E2%BF%93#Translingual" title="⿓">
          ⿓
         </a>
        </i>

       </li>

           (Min Nan)
          </span>
         </li>
         <li>
          <b class="Hani" lang="zh">
           <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/wuu:%E9%BE%99" title="w:wuu:龙">
            龙
           </a>
          </b>
          <span style="font-size:80%">
           (Wu)
          </span>
         </li>
        </ul>
       </div>
      </div>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Glyph_origin">
        Glyph origin
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">

             </span>
            </small>

      </div>
      <p>
       Pictogram (
       <i class="Hani mention" lang="zh">
        <a href="/wiki/%E8%B1%A1%E5%BD%A2#Chinese" title="象形">
         象形
        </a>
       </i>
       ) – originally a serpent with prominent whiskered mouth and eyes.
      </p>
      <p>
       Current form developed in large seal script, with serpent’s body on right (tail at upper right, legs on right), whiskered/fanged mouth at lower left, and eyes/crown at upper left. Left side was subsequently simplified and abstracted, with some influence of
       <span class="Hani" lang="zh">
        <a href="/wiki/%E7%AB%8B#Chinese" title="立">
         立
        </a>
       </span>
       and
       <span class="Hani" lang="zh">
        <a href="/wiki/%E2%BA%BC#Chinese" title="⺼">
         ⺼
        </a>
       </span>
       /
       <span class="Hani" lang="zh">
        <a href="/wiki/%E6%9C%88#Chinese" title="月">
         月
        </a>
       </span>
       . Note that
       <span class="Hani" lang="zh">
        <a href="/wiki/%E7%AB%9C#Chinese" title="竜">
         竜
        </a>
       </span>
       existed as a traditional variant dating back to large seal script, and figures a dragon seen face-on, rather than curled around.
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">
        Etymology
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%BE%8D&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Etymology">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       From
       <span class="etyl">
        <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sino-Tibetan_languages" title="w:Sino-Tibetan languages">
         Proto-Sino-Tibetan
        </a>
       </span>
       <i class="Latn mention" lang="sit-pro">
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Sino-Tibetan/m-bru(%C5%8B/k)" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Sino-Tibetan/m-bru(ŋ/k)">
         *m-bru(ŋ/k)
        </a>
       </i>
       <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">
        (
       </span>
       <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">
        “
       </span>
       <span class="mention-gloss">
        dragon; thunder
       </span>
       <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">
        ”
       </span>
       <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">
        )
       </span>
       . Cognate with
       <span class="etyl">
        <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lhasa_Tibetan" title="w:Lhasa Tibetan">
         Tibetan
        </a>
       </span>
       <i class="Tibt mention" lang="bo">
        <a href="/wiki/%E0%BD%A0%E0%BD%96%E0%BE%B2%E0%BD%B4%E0%BD%82#Tibetan" title="འབྲུག">
         འབྲུག
        </a>
       </i>
       <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">
        (
       </span>
       <span class="mention-tr tr Latn" lang="bo-Latn">
        'brug
       </span>
       ,
       <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">
        “
       </span>
       <span class="mention-gloss">
        dragon; thunder
       </span>
       <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">
        ”
       </span>
       <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">
        )
       </span>
       . The STEDT database also lists
       <span class="Hani" lang="zh">
        <a href="/wiki/%E9%9A%86#Chinese" title="隆">
         隆
        </a>
       </span>
       (
       <i>
        <span class="tr Latn">
         <span style="border-bottom: 1px dotted 000; cursor:help" title="Old Chinese">
          OC
         </span>
         *ɡ·ruːŋ
        </span>
       </i>
       , “thunder; sound of thunder”) and
       <span class="Hani" lang="zh">
        <a href="/wiki/%E9%9B%B9#Chinese" title="雹">
         雹
        </a>
       </span>
       (
       <i>
        <span class="tr Latn">
         <span style="border-bottom: 1px dotted 000; cursor:help" title="Old Chinese">
          OC
         </span>
         *bruːɡ
        </span>
       </i>
       , “hail”) as cognates. Also compare
       <span class="Hani" lang="zh">
        <a href="/wiki/%E9%9D%90#Chinese" title="靐">
         靐
        </a>
       </span>
       (
       <i>
        <span class="tr Latn">
         <span style="border-bottom: 1px dotted 000; cursor:help" title="Old Chinese">
          OC
         </span>
         *brɯŋs
        </span>
       </i>
       , “sound of thunder”) and
       <span class="Hant" lang="zh-Hant">
        <a href="/wiki/%E9%9C%B9%E9%9D%82#Chinese" title="霹靂">
         霹靂
        </a>
       </span>
       (
       <i>
        <span class="tr Latn">
         <span style="border-bottom: 1px dotted 000; cursor:help" title="Old Chinese">
          OC
         </span>
         *pʰeːɡ reːɡ
        </span>
       </i>
       , “thunder”).
      </p>
      <p>
       This word is found in many languages of the region. Compare
       <span class="etyl">
        <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Hmong%E2%80%93Mien_language" title="w:Proto-Hmong–Mien language">
         Proto-Hmong-Mien
        </a>
       </span>
       <i class="Latinx mention" lang="hmx-pro">
        <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Hmong-Mien/-ro%C5%8B&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Hmong-Mien/-roŋ (page does not exist)">
         *-roŋ
        </a>
       </i>
       <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">
        (
       </span>
       <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">
        “
       </span>
       <span class="mention-gloss">
        dragon
       </span>
       <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">
        ”
       </span>
       <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">
        )
       </span>
       (
       <span class="etyl">
        <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/White_Hmong_language" title="w:White Hmong language">
         White Hmong
        </a>
       </span>
       <i class="Latn mention" lang="mww">
        <a href="/wiki/zaj#White_Hmong" title="zaj">
         zaj
        </a>
       </i>
       ),
       <span class="etyl">
        <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Vietic_language" title="w:Proto-Vietic language">
         Proto-Vietic
        </a>
       </span>
       <i class="Latinx mention" lang="mkh-vie-pro">
        <a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Vietic/-ro%CB%90%C5%8B" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Vietic/-roːŋ">
         *-roːŋ
        </a>
       </i>
       <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">
        (
       </span>
       <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">
        “
       </span>
       <span class="mention-gloss">
        dragon
       </span>
       <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">
        ”
       </span>
       <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">
        )
       </span>
       (
       <span class="etyl">
        <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vietnamese_language" title="w:Vietnamese language">
         Vietnamese
        </a>
       </span>
       <i class="Latn mention" lang="vi">
        <a href="/wiki/r%E1%BB%93ng#Vietnamese" title="rồng">
         rồng
        </a>
       </i>
       ),
       <span class="etyl">
        <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vietnamese_language" title="w:Vietnamese language">
         Vietnamese
        </a>
       </span>
       <i class="Latn mention" lang="vi">
        <a href="/wiki/thu%E1%BB%93ng_lu%E1%BB%93ng#Vietnamese" title="thuồng luồng">
         <b>
          th
         </b>
         uồng
         <b>
          luồng
         </b>
        </a>
       </i>
       <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">
        (
       </span>
       <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">
        “
       </span>
       <span class="mention-gloss">
        serpent-like monster
       </span>
       <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">
        ”
       </span>
       <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">
        )
       </span>
       ,
       <span class="etyl">
        <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Khmer_language" title="w:Khmer language">
         Khmer
        </a>
       </span>
       <i class="Khmr mention" lang="km">
        <a href="/wiki/%E1%9E%9A%E1%9F%84%E1%9E%84#Khmer" title="រោង">
         រោង
        </a>
       </i>
       <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">
        (
       </span>
       <span class="mention-tr tr Latn" lang="km-Latn">
        roong
       </span>
       ,
       <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">
        “

       <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">

       <span class="etyl">
        <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Thai_language" title="w:Thai language">
         Thai
        </a>
       </span>
       <i class="Thai mention" lang="th">
        <a href="/wiki/%E0%B8%A1%E0%B8%B0%E0%B9%82%E0%B8%A3%E0%B8%87#Thai" title="มะโรง">

        </a>
       </i>
       <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">

       </span>
       <span class="mention-tr tr Latn" lang="th-Latn">

       <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">

       </span>

       <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">

       <span class="etyl">

       </span>
       <small>
        [script needed]
       </small>

        </a>

        </a>

         <div style="border: 1px solid green; padding: 4px; margin: 8px; background: #F7F4ED; font-size: 85%">
          <b>
           Note
          </b>
          :
          <ul>
           <li>
            lṳ̀ng - literary;
           </li>
           <li>
            lèng - vernacular (only used in
            <span class="Hant" lang="zh-Hant">
             <a href="/wiki/%E9%BE%8D%E7%9C%BC#Chinese" title="龍眼">
              龍眼
             </a>
            </span>
            );
           </li>
           <li>
            liòng &gt; lùng - literary (only used in
            <span class="Hant" lang="zh-Hant">
             <a href="/wiki/%E9%BE%8D%E8%88%B9#Chinese" title="龍船">
              龍船
             </a>
            </span>
            ).

             <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=ulug%27&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="ulug' (page does not exist)">

             </a>

            <link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r68481116" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/>
           </li>

            <span class="ug-Arab" lang="ug">
             <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%D8%A6%DB%87%D9%84%DB%87%D8%BA&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="ئۇلۇغ (page does not exist)">
              ئۇلۇغ
             </a>

      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">
        Usage notes
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%BE%8D&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Usage notes">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h4>
      <ul>
       <li>
        This kanji is the
        <i class="Jpan mention" lang="ja">
         <a href="/wiki/%E6%97%A7%E5%AD%97%E4%BD%93#Japanese" title="旧字体">
          旧字体
         </a>
        </i>
        <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">
         (
        </span>
        <span class="mention-tr tr">
         <a href="/wiki/ky%C5%ABjitai" title="kyūjitai">
          kyūjitai
         </a>
        </span>
        <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">
         )
        </span>
        form of simplified
        <i class="Jpan mention" lang="ja">
         <a href="/wiki/%E7%AB%9C#Japanese" title="竜">
          竜
         </a>
        </i>
        , itself as isolated
        <i class="Jpan mention" lang="ja">
         <a href="/wiki/%E6%96%B0%E5%AD%97%E4%BD%93#Japanese" title="新字体">
          新字体
         </a>
        </i>
        <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">
         (
        </span>
        <span class="mention-tr tr">
         <a href="/wiki/shinjitai" title="shinjitai">
          shinjitai
         </a>
        </span>
        <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">
         )
        </span>
        kanji, but is used in Jōyō characters
        <i class="Jpan mention" lang="ja">
         <a href="/wiki/%E8%A5%B2#Japanese" title="襲">
          襲
         </a>
        </i>
        and
        <i class="Jpan mention" lang="ja">
         <a href="/wiki/%E7%B1%A0#Japanese" title="籠">
          籠
         </a>
        </i>
        , with the latter categorized as Jōyō as of 2010.
       </li>
       <li>
        Although it is officially simplified into
        <i class="Jpan mention" lang="ja">
         <a href="/wiki/%E7%AB%9C#Japanese" title="竜">
          竜
         </a>
        </i>
        ,
        <i class="Jpan mention" lang="ja">
         龍
        </i>
        is often used instead for certain words for its aesthetics (such as in literary contexts or for spelling words borrowed from Chinese). For example,
        <i class="Jpan mention" lang="ja">
         <a href="/wiki/%E7%83%8F%E9%BE%8D%E8%8C%B6#Japanese" title="烏龍茶">
          烏龍茶
         </a>
        </i>
        <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">
         (
        </span>
        <span class="mention-tr tr">
         ūroncha
        </span>
        ,
        <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">
         “
        </span>
        <span class="mention-gloss">
         <a href="/wiki/oolong_tea" title="oolong tea">
          oolong tea
         </a>
        </span>
        <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">
         ”
        </span>
        <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">
         )
        </span>
        is rarely spelled as
        <i class="Jpan mention" lang="ja">
         <a href="/wiki/%E7%83%8F%E7%AB%9C%E8%8C%B6#Japanese" title="烏竜茶">
          烏竜茶
         </a>
        </i>
        .
       </li>
      </ul>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">
        Etymology 1
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%BE%8D&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Etymology 1">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <table class="wikitable kanji-table" style="text-align: center; font-size: small; float: right;">
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th style="font-weight: normal;">
          <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Japanese_glossary#kanji" title="Appendix:Japanese glossary">
           Kanji
          </a>
          in this term
         </th>
        </tr>
        <tr class="Jpan" lang="ja" style="font-size: 2em; background: white; line-height: 1em;">
         <td style="padding: 0.5em;">
          <a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Japanese">
           龍
          </a>
         </td>
        </tr>
        <tr style="background: white;">
         <td>
          <span class="Jpan" lang="ja">
           りゅう
          </span>
          <br/>
          <small>
           <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Japanese_glossary#jinmeiyō_kanji" title="Appendix:Japanese glossary">
            Jinmeiyō
           </a>
          </small>
         </td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
         <td colspan="1">
          <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Japanese_glossary#goon" title="Appendix:Japanese glossary">
           goon
          </a>
         </td>
        </tr>
       </tbody>
      </table>
      <table class="wikitable floatright">
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th style="font-weight:normal">
          Alternative spelling
         </th>
        </tr>
        <tr>
         <td style="text-align:center;font-size:108%">
          <span class="Jpan" lang="ja" style="font-size:140%">
           <a href="/wiki/%E7%AB%9C#Japanese" title="竜">
            竜
           </a>
          </span>
         </td>
        </tr>
       </tbody>
      </table>
      <p>
       From
       <span class="etyl">
        <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Chinese" title="w:Middle Chinese">
         Middle Chinese
        </a>
       </span>
       <span class="Hant" lang="zh-Hant">
        <a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Chinese">
         龍
        </a>
       </span>
       (
       <i>
        <span class="tr Latn">
         <span style="border-bottom: 1px dotted 000; cursor:help" title="Middle Chinese">
          MC
         </span>
         lɨoŋ
        </span>
       </i>
       ).
      </p>
      <p>
       The
       <i class="Jpan mention" lang="ja">
        <a href="/wiki/%E5%91%89%E9%9F%B3#Japanese" title="呉音">
         呉音
        </a>
       </i>
       <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">
        (
       </span>
       <span class="mention-tr tr">
        goon
       </span>
       , literally
       <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">
        “
       </span>
       <span class="mention-gloss">
        <a href="/wiki/Wu" title="Wu">
         Wu
        </a>
        <a href="/wiki/sound" title="sound">
         sound
        </a>
       </span>
       <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">
        ”
       </span>
       <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">
        )
       </span>
       reading, so likely the initial borrowing from
       <span class="etyl">
        <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Chinese" title="w:Middle Chinese">
         Middle Chinese
        </a>
       </span>
       .
      </p>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_2">
        Pronunciation
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%BE%8D&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h4>
      <ul>
       <li>
        <a href="/wiki/%E9%9F%B3%E8%AA%AD%E3%81%BF#Japanese" title="音読み">
         On’yomi
        </a>
        :
        <a href="/wiki/%E5%91%89%E9%9F%B3#Japanese" title="呉音">
         Goon
        </a>
       </li>
       <ul>
        <li>
         <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">
          (
         </span>
         <span class="ib-content qualifier-content">
          <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tokyo_dialect" title="w:Tokyo dialect">
           Tokyo
          </a>
         </span>
         <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">
          )
         </span>
         <span class="Jpan" lang="ja">
          <span style="border-top:1px solid black;position:relative;padding:1px;">
           りゅ
           <span style="position:absolute;top:0;bottom:67%;right:0%;border-right:1px solid black;">
            ​
           </span>
          </span>
          う
         </span>
         <span class="Latn">
          <samp>
           [ryúꜜù]
          </samp>
         </span>
         (
         <a href="/wiki/%E9%A0%AD%E9%AB%98%E5%9E%8B" title="頭高型">
          Atamadaka
         </a>
         – [1])
         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-DJR_1-0">
          <a href="#cite_note-DJR-1">
           [1]
          </a>
         </sup>
        </li>
        <li>
         <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">
          IPA
         </a>
         <sup>
          (
          <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Japanese_pronunciation" title="Appendix:Japanese pronunciation">
           key
          </a>
          )
         </sup>
         :
         <span class="IPA">
          [ɾʲɨᵝː]
         </span>
        </li>
       </ul>
      </ul>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Some dictionaries classify this reading as
        <i class="Jpan mention" lang="ja">
         <a href="/wiki/%E6%85%A3%E7%94%A8%E9%9F%B3#Japanese" title="慣用音">
          慣用音
         </a>
        </i>
        <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">
         (
        </span>
        <span class="mention-tr tr">
         kanyōon
        </span>
        , literally
        <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">
         “
        </span>
        <span class="mention-gloss">
         <a href="/wiki/common" title="common">
          commonly
         </a>
         -
         <a href="/wiki/accepted" title="accepted">
          accepted
         </a>
         sound
        </span>
        <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">
         ”
        </span>
        <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">
         )
        </span>
        instead of
        <i class="Jpan mention" lang="ja">
         呉音
        </i>
        <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">
         (
        </span>
        <span class="mention-tr tr">
         goon
        </span>
        <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">
         )
        </span>
        .
       </li>
      </ul>

      <p>
       From
       <span class="etyl">
        <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Chinese" title="w:Middle Chinese">
         Middle Chinese
        </a>
       </span>
       <span class="Hant" lang="zh-Hant">
        <a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Chinese">
         龍
        </a>
       </span>
       (
       <i>
        <span class="tr Latn">
         <span style="border-bottom: 1px dotted 000; cursor:help" title="Middle Chinese">
          MC
         </span>
         lɨoŋ
        </span>
       </i>
       ).
      </p>
      <p>
       The
       <i class="Jpan mention" lang="ja">
        <a href="/wiki/%E6%BC%A2%E9%9F%B3#Japanese" title="漢音">
         漢音
        </a>
       </i>
       <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">
        (
       </span>
       <span class="mention-tr tr">
        kan'on
       </span>
       , literally
       <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">
        “
       </span>
       <span class="mention-gloss">
        <a href="/wiki/Han" title="Han">
         Han
        </a>
        <a href="/wiki/sound" title="sound">
         sound
        </a>
       </span>
       <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">
        ”
       </span>
       <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">
        )
       </span>
       reading, so likely a later borrowing from
       <span class="etyl">
        <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Chinese" title="w:Middle Chinese">
         Middle Chinese
        </a>
       </span>
       .
      </p>

      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">
        Etymology
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%BE%8D&amp;action=edit&amp;section=39" title="Edit section: Etymology">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       From
       <span class="etyl">
        <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Chinese" title="w:Middle Chinese">
         Middle Chinese
        </a>
       </span>
       <span class="Hant" lang="zh-Hant">
        <a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Chinese">
         龍
        </a>
       </span>
       (
       <i>
        <span class="tr Latn">
         <span style="border-bottom: 1px dotted 000; cursor:help" title="Middle Chinese">
          MC
         </span>
         lɨoŋ
        </span>
       </i>
       ). Recorded as
       <a href="/wiki/Middle_Korean" title="Middle Korean">
        Middle Korean
       </a>
       <i class="Kore mention" lang="okm">
        <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%EB%A3%8C%E1%87%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="료ᇰ (page does not exist)">
         료ᇰ
        </a>
       </i>
       <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">
        (
       </span>
       <span class="mention-tr tr Latn" lang="okm-Latn">
        lyong
       </span>
       <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">
        )
       </span>
       (
       <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yale_romanization_of_Korean" title="w:Yale romanization of Korean">
        Yale
       </a>
       :
       <i>
        lyong
       </i>
       ) in
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/%ED%9B%88%EB%AA%BD%EC%9E%90%ED%9A%8C" title="훈몽자회">
         Hunmong Jahoe
        </a>
       </i>
       (
       <span class="Kore" lang="ko">
        <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ko:s:%ED%9B%88%EB%AA%BD%EC%9E%90%ED%9A%8C/%E9%B1%97%E4%BB%8B#상20A" title="w:ko:s:훈몽자회/鱗介">
         訓蒙字會 / 훈몽자회
        </a>
       </span>
       ), 1527.
      </p>

      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">
        Etymology
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%BE%8D&amp;action=edit&amp;section=45" title="Edit section: Etymology">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       Possibly from the verb
       <i class="Jpan mention" lang="ja">
        <a href="/wiki/%E7%AB%8B%E3%81%A4#Japanese" title="立つ">
         立つ
        </a>
       </i>
       <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">
        (
       </span>
       <span class="mention-tr tr">
        tatu
       </span>
       ,
       <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">
        “
       </span>
       <span class="mention-gloss">
        to
        <a href="/wiki/rise" title="rise">
         rise
        </a>
        ,
        <a href="/wiki/stand" title="stand">
         stand
        </a>
       </span>
       <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">
        ”
       </span>
       <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">
        )
       </span>
       .
      </p>

       <strong class="Jpan headword" lang="ojp">
        龍
       </strong>
       (

        tatu
       </span>
       ) (
       <i>
        kana
       </i>

         edit

        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h4>
      <p>
       Also used once phonetically as a
       <i class="Jpan mention" lang="ja">
        <a href="/wiki/%E5%80%9F%E8%A8%93#Japanese" title="借訓">
         借訓
        </a>
       </i>
       <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">
        (
       </span>
       <span class="mention-tr tr">
        shakkun
       </span>
       <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">
        )
       </span>
       for
       <span class="IPA">
        ⟨tatu⟩
       </span>
       .
      </p>

      <hr/>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Pai-lang">
        Pai-lang
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%BE%8D&amp;action=edit&amp;section=50" title="Edit section: Pai-lang">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_6">
        Etymology
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%BE%8D&amp;action=edit&amp;section=51" title="Edit section: Etymology">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       Coblin, reconstructing the Pai-lang pronunciation as *
       <i>
        gljung
       </i>
       , suggests that it derives from
       <span class="etyl">
        <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sino-Tibetan_languages" title="w:Sino-Tibetan languages">
         Proto-Sino-Tibetan
        </a>
       </span>
       <i class="Latn mention" lang="sit-pro">
        <a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Sino-Tibetan/kl(j)u(%C5%8B/k)" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Sino-Tibetan/kl(j)u(ŋ/k)">
         *kl(j)u(ŋ/k)
        </a>
       </i>
       <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">
        (
       </span>
       <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">
        “
       </span>
       <span class="mention-gloss">
        river, gorge
       </span>
       <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">
        ”
       </span>
       <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">
        )
       </span>
       and retains its consonant cluster, which was lost in
       <span class="etyl">
        <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Lolo-Burmese_language" title="w:Proto-Lolo-Burmese language">
         Proto-Lolo-Burmese
        </a>
       </span>
       . Compare
       <span class="etyl">
        <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lhasa_Tibetan" title="w:Lhasa Tibetan">
         Tibetan
        </a>
       </span>
       <i class="Tibt mention" lang="bo">
        <a href="/wiki/%E0%BD%A3%E0%BE%97%E0%BD%BC%E0%BD%84%E0%BD%A6#Tibetan" title="ལྗོངས">
         ལྗོངས
        </a>
       </i>
       <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">
        (
       </span>
       <span class="mention-tr tr Latn" lang="bo-Latn">
        ljongs
       </span>
       <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">
        )
       </span>
       ,
       <span class="etyl">
        <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chinese_language" title="w:Chinese language">
         Chinese
        </a>
       </span>
       <span class="Hani" lang="zh">
        <a href="/wiki/%E8%B0%B7#Chinese" title="谷">
         谷
        </a>
       </span>
       (
       <i>
        <span class="tr Latn">
         <span style="border-bottom: 1px dotted 000; cursor:help" title="Old Chinese">
          OC
         </span>
         *kloːɡ
        </span>
       </i>
       ).
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">
        Noun
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%BE%8D&amp;action=edit&amp;section=52" title="Edit section: Noun">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       <strong class="Hani headword" lang="tbq-plg">
        龍
       </strong>
       (
       <span class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr" lang="tbq-plg-Latn">
        *gljung
       </span>
       )
      </p>
      <ol>
       <li>
        <a href="/wiki/gorge" title="gorge">
         gorge
        </a>
       </li>
      </ol>

       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
